<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> one (35)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Hoofdtelwoord"><i>Hoofdtelwoord</i></span></h4>
<p><b>one</b>
</p>
<ol><li>één
<dl><dd>«There <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> only <b>one</b> president at the time»
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>Er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:altijd.html>altijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <b>één</b> president <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ieder.html>ieder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gegeven.html>gegeven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a>.</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ongedekt.html>ongedekt</a> (41817)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ongedect</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">on-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gedekt.html>gedekt</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ongedekt.html>ongedekt</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>uncovered, not protected against attacks or the elements</li>
<li>uncovered, not wearing headwear</li>
<li>naked, not clothed</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of female animals</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> uncovered, not having <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> covered by a male animal</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">finance</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> unsecured</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">linguistics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> unchecked, being in an open syllable</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of tables</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> not covered by a tablecloth</li></ol>

***ongelijk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ongelijk.html>ongelijk</a> (4696)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ungilīk</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ungalīkaz</i>; surface analysis: <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">on-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">un-</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelijk.html>gelijk</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">equal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">unġelīċ</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">unlike</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">ungleich</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">úlíkr</i> <i>(see there for North Germanic descendants)</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ongelijk.html>ongelijk</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ongelijk.html>ongelijker</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">ongelijkst</b>)

<ol><li>unequal, different</li>
<li>uneven, rough, <a href = vnd.unilang:bumpy.html>bumpy</a></li></ol>

***ongeluk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ongeluk.html>ongeluk</a> (788)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ongeluc</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">on-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geluk.html>geluk</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ongeluk.html>ongeluk</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ongelukken.html>ongelukken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ongelukje.html>ongelukje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>unhappiness, misery</li>
<li>accident</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bad luck, misfortune</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***ongesteld.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ongesteld.html>ongesteld</a> (9458)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ongestelt</i>. The sense “menstruating” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a relatively recent development that originated as a euphemism.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ongesteld.html>ongesteld</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">menstruating</span> <span class="defdate">[from late 19th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1894</b>, A. N. Nolst Trenité, <i>Handboek <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> ziekenverpleging</i>, publ. by J. H. amp; G. <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Heteren, page 74.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ongeval.html>ongeval</a> (5552)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ongeval.html>ongeval</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">on-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geval.html>geval</a></i>. Cf. <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Unfall</i>.

***onmiddellijk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:onmiddellijk.html>onmiddellijk</a> (1395)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>17th century, loan translation of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">immediatus</i>, perhaps after <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">unmittelbar</i> (older also <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">unmittelich</i>). Analysable as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">on-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">un-</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:middel.html>middel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">means, medium</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onmiddellijk.html>onmiddellijk</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
